# CollectiveEventTwin 完整项目原子任务级开发计划 / canonical production plan v1.0

Date: 2026-05-09
Status: single execution entry, full atomic development ledger, UTF-8 with BOM for Windows editors.

This document supersedes parallel implementation-plan/backlog files. Historical docs remain source material only. Execution, validation, and progress reporting must use this file.

Critical correction: the earlier S8 PASS is revoked. Frontend production pages are not frozen while core routes still rely on generic StructuredPage rendering or route smoke tests only.

Numbering note: the old source has no AT-344 through AT-359. These IDs are intentionally not reused here.

## 2. Non-negotiable execution constraints

1. No frontend mock product data. No static fixture as product data source. No frontend-only business state.
2. All product data comes from PostgreSQL and is returned by FastAPI.
3. Every meaningful frontend action must call a backend API, workflow, or activity and must write audit where it mutates state.
4. Agent, LLM, algorithm, report, task, evidence, and review outputs must have database records and evidence/input references.
5. Synthetic data is allowed only when explicitly labeled and only through the real ingestion-cleaning-extraction-storage-algorithm-Agent-report chain.
6. Static design pages are visual/product-flow baselines only. React pages must implement the body visually from the static design first, keep the city-situation header style, and use Chinese menu labels.
7. StructuredPage is a temporary fallback only and cannot be used as a freeze criterion.
8. Every atomic task must pass functional, exception, business, performance, browser, and third-party review checks before freeze.

## 3. Current true status

| Area | True status | Required correction |
| --- | --- | --- |
| backend/API/DB | Implemented through much of S7B, but old AT gaps remain for adapters, channels, parsers, full multimedia, professional agents, PDF/DOCX, and independent review gates. | Revalidate every implemented item against this ledger before freezing. |
| frontend | City is relatively complete; S1/S2 consoles exist; most product pages still need production page implementation and full state matrix. | Restart at FE-S1 and freeze page by page. |
| OpenAPI/DTO | packages/contracts/openapi/v1.0.yaml exists but must track this full ledger. | Update contract before backend/frontend changes. |
| Alembic | 0001-0013 exist; 0014+ must carry index/constraint/view and old AT gap tables. | Never reorder existing revisions. |
| testing/browser | Backend tests exist; frontend browser/state/visual evidence is insufficient. | Add real click, network, console, screenshots, and review records for every freeze point. |

### 3.1 Page-first extraction baseline

Correction: frontend function count and backend API count cannot be finalized from historical plans alone. The execution ledger must be driven by static page assets, React implementation, OpenAPI, and FastAPI routes together.

Machine extraction snapshot on 2026-05-09:

| Source | Count / evidence | Planning impact |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Static HTML pages under `worldline-observer-current` | 11 pages inspected: 243 buttons, 108 links, 13 inputs, 2 selects, 366 interactive elements total | This is the minimum page-action discovery baseline; navigation and decorative buttons must be separated from business actions before implementation. |
| Static page JavaScript event handlers | Event listeners detected in `city-monitor.html`, `data-hub.html`, `mainline-builder.html`, `worldline-observer.html`, `agent-council.html`, `decision-brief.html`, `event-detail-evidence.html` | Interactions implemented in static JS must be converted into React state plus real API calls, not copied as frontend-only behavior. |
| Design assets | `design/设计稿/城市感知态势.png`, `design/设计稿/主题态势驾驶舱.png`, plus static HTML pages | Page body must follow the design/static baseline first; header keeps the city-situation style and Chinese menu labels. |
| React implementation | Product route still has `StructuredPage` fallback; 11 product page literals detected | Any page still using generic rendering cannot be frozen. |
| OpenAPI contract | `packages/contracts/openapi/v1.0.yaml` has 168 paths and 190 operations | API count must be reconciled with page-action requirements; unused or missing operations must be marked before coding. |
| FastAPI implementation | `apps/api/src/worldline_api/main.py` registers about 192 route handlers | Implementation count must be reconciled with OpenAPI and page actions; route presence alone does not prove page coverage. |
| Web API client | `apps/web/src/api.ts` currently exposes far fewer direct request templates than OpenAPI routes | Frontend API client coverage is a known gap and must be expanded page by page. |

Therefore, section 9 is a starting execution ledger, not the final page-derived action contract. Before each page implementation begins, the corresponding static page must be decomposed into: visual regions, user actions, system actions, API queries, API mutations, DB writes, algorithms/Agent calls, state matrix, browser checks, and third-party review records.

## 4. Frontend page ledger

| Domain | Route | Page | Static/design baseline | Atomic interactions |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| foundation | /login | login/session | none | auth success/failure, disabled, locked, refresh, logout |
| foundation | /admin?tab=users | users/roles | none | list, create, edit role, disable, permission diff |
| foundation | /admin?tab=audit | audit center | none | filter, detail, object trace |
| foundation | /admin?tab=reviews | review/gate | none | create, pass, fail, waive, gate-check, retest |
| foundation | /admin?tab=ops | ops health | none | api/db/worker, workflow, error queue, retry queue, metrics |
| data | /admin?tab=sources | source governance | worldline-observer-current/data-source-model-config.html | source CRUD, policy-check, run control, retry, quality |
| product | /cases/:caseId/city | city situation | design/设计稿/城市感知态势.png; worldline-observer-current/city-monitor.html | city switch, layer, rank, filter, detail, health, media, timeline, create topic |
| product | /cases/:caseId/risk | topic situation | design/设计稿/主题态势驾驶舱.png; worldline-observer-current/risk-dashboard.html | topic list, scope edit, trend, spread, stance, candidate mainline |
| product | /cases/:caseId/data | data/signal workbench | worldline-observer-current/data-hub.html | raw search, lineage, extraction run, signal package |
| product | /cases/:caseId/evidence | evidence review | worldline-observer-current/event-detail-evidence.html | candidate, review, attachment, risk factor, media link, redaction |
| product | /cases/:caseId/mainline | mainline builder | worldline-observer-current/mainline-builder.html | draft, node/edge edit, layout save, quality, confirm, stakeholder review |
| product | /cases/:caseId/worldline | worldline simulation | worldline-observer-current/worldline-observer.html | run, result, intervention, rerun, compare, explain, send council |
| product | /cases/:caseId/council | agent council | worldline-observer-current/agent-council.html | profile readiness, council run, guardrail, apply result |
| product | /cases/:caseId/brief | brief/report | worldline-observer-current/decision-brief.html | generate, edit, validate, approve, publish, export, tasks |
| product | /cases/:caseId/memory | retrospective | worldline-observer-current/case-memory.html | create retrospective, metrics, knowledge item, approve, publish |
| product | /cases/:caseId/library | case library | worldline-observer-current/topic-case-library.html | search, detail, semantic recall, apply, conflict |
| product | /cases/:caseId/config | config center | worldline-observer-current/data-source-model-config.html | version, taxonomy, algorithm params, agent/prompt, regression, approval, publish, rollback, impact |

Each page must cover loading, empty, error, degraded, no permission, normal, selected, submitting, success, failure, 409 conflict, 403 forbidden, and dependency-degraded states. Freeze requires desktop screenshot, mobile screenshot, network log, console log, browser click record, and third-party review record.

### 4.1 Map capability ledger

The City page map is a product capability, not a decorative background. Business facts, event geometry, heat scores, clusters, layers, and selected event details must come from PostgreSQL through FastAPI. The map SDK may render tiles and camera movement, but it cannot become the source of product truth.

| Capability | Frontend requirement | Backend/API requirement | DB / persistence | Test and freeze requirement |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Base map render | Render real map container with map/satellite/heat modes and local fallback when tiles fail | `GET /api/v1/cities/{city_id}/map-config` returns provider, center, zoom, bounds, tile health, fallback style | `city_map_states`, `map_provider_status` | Browser screenshot with normal tiles and forced tile failure; console has no React error |
| Viewport and camera | Zoom in, zoom out, home, pan, fit bounds, restore last view | `PATCH /api/v1/cities/{city_id}/map-state` persists center, zoom, mode, bounds, layer state | `city_map_states`, audit log | Refresh keeps persisted state; unauthorized city returns 403 |
| Layer control | Toggle event layers, source layers, risk layers, heat opacity, layer search, panel collapse | `GET /api/v1/cities/{city_id}/map-layers`; `PATCH /api/v1/cities/{city_id}/map-state` | `city_map_states`, `source_health`, `city_events` | Layer toggle changes only visible rendering, not business facts; state reloads from API |
| Event markers | Render points from API with risk tone, source, time, synthetic flag, permission masking | `GET /api/v1/cities/{city_id}/map-events` or `map-layers` returns event features | `city_events`, `signals`, `evidence`, `lineage_edges` | Marker click opens same event as rank/timeline; masked events cannot leak hidden fields |
| Zoom-dependent clustering | Cluster and split points by zoom and density, preserving risk rollups and event counts | Backend returns cluster policy/version or precomputed clusters when needed | `city_events`, optional `city_event_clusters` | Pixel/browser check at multiple zoom levels; no marker overlap explosion |
| Heat layer | Render heat intensity from backend score, not frontend random values | `GET /api/v1/cities/{city_id}/heat-layer` returns cells/features, score_version, input_refs | `algorithm_runs`, `city_events`, `risk_factors` | Heat score is reproducible by algorithm version; degraded state when score is stale |
| POI and region overlays | Render district/POI labels, key zones, routes, and warning areas | `GET /api/v1/cities/{city_id}/overlays` | `city_overlays` or versioned config rows | Empty overlay state and permission filtering covered |
| Event selection sync | Map marker, rank row, timeline dot/card, material list, and detail drawer share selected event | `GET /api/v1/city-events/{event_id}`; optional `POST /api/v1/city-events/{event_id}/selection-events` for audited business selection | `city_events`, `audit_logs` when selection is persisted | Real click test across marker/rank/timeline/media; URL or persisted selection stays consistent |
| Map-to-workflow actions | From selected event create topic, join mainline, open data, send evidence review, mark confirmed/review/noise | Existing or new mutation endpoints for topic/mainline/evidence/status actions | `topics`, `mainlines`, `evidence_reviews`, `city_events`, `audit_logs` | Every button calls API; no toast-only business outcome |
| Performance | Keep map interaction responsive with many events and media markers | API supports viewport bounds, pagination, clustering, ETag/cache metadata | indexed geometry/bounds fields, materialized views if needed | 1k events p95 API and browser frame budget recorded |

### 4.2 Page-action omission audit

Readable rule: one atomic task equals one user action or one system action that changes business scope, selection, persisted state, workflow state, generated conclusion, export, approval, review, retry, or configuration version. Pure navigation and visual-only decoration may be grouped, but every grouped action must be listed in the page contract and proved by browser/network evidence. Each row in section 9 must be readable as: who clicks or which system action runs, which API/workflow is called, which database record changes or is read, which algorithm/Agent participates if any, and how the result is tested.

| Static/design page | Extracted business actions | Previous gap | New required atomic rows |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `city-monitor.html` | 59 buttons, 3 inputs, 1 select: time ranges, map controls, layers, event filters, search, marker/rank/timeline/media selection, panel collapse, copy/share-like actions | Map rows were added, but non-map City toolbar and persisted selection state were still too broad | `S3A-PAGE-001` to `S3A-PAGE-005` |
| `risk-dashboard.html` | 9 buttons, 1 select, many route links: time window, topic filters, trend/spread/stance drilldown, candidate mainline entry | Topic page had only coarse APIs and did not pin per-filter/per-snapshot actions | `S3B-PAGE-001` to `S3B-PAGE-005` |
| `data-hub.html` | 22 buttons, 7 inputs, 2 selects: search, pagination, row detail, keyword/tag filtering, similar-data search, continue data supplement, add to mainline draft | Search and signal package existed, but workbench UI operations were not atomic enough | `S4A-PAGE-001` to `S4A-PAGE-007` |
| `event-detail-evidence.html` | 9 buttons: evidence tabs, chain view, risk score, manual review, confirm into simulation, adjust risk, return to observation | Evidence review existed, but page tabs and status-changing actions were missing | `S4B-PAGE-001` to `S4B-PAGE-005` |
| `mainline-builder.html` | 67 buttons, 3 inputs: clue boxes, tag/time filters, candidate switch, graph node selection, suggestion drawer actions, evidence supplement, confirm with gaps, layout fit | Mainline was defined as a module, but the builder's graph and drawer actions were not split to button-level tasks | `S5-PAGE-001` to `S5-PAGE-010` |
| `worldline-observer.html` | 25 buttons: play/pause, previous/next, step selection, node tabs, interventions, continue as hypothesis, start Council | Worldline run existed, but simulation playback and intervention UI state were under-specified | `S6-WORLDLINE-UI-001` to `S6-WORLDLINE-UI-005` |
| `agent-council.html` | 7 buttons: next round, pressure test, inject result and rerun, save judgment, generated profile/result detail buttons | Council existed, but round operation and pressure-test/apply-result actions were not separate enough | `S6-COUNCIL-UI-001` to `S6-COUNCIL-UI-004` |
| `decision-brief.html` | 6 buttons: export, return to mainline, batch export, create task, single export, update task | Report generation existed, but report task and export runtime states were missing | `S7A-PAGE-001` to `S7A-PAGE-005` |
| `case-memory.html` | 15 buttons: retrospective tabs, draft, submit review, confirm into knowledge base, export sample, view/execute actions | Retrospective existed, but its review and model-update loop was too coarse | `S7B-MEMORY-001` to `S7B-MEMORY-005` |
| `topic-case-library.html` | 32 buttons, 1 input: create case, category filters, library tabs, sort, open, apply, write back, add to topic, apply to simulation | Case search existed, but apply/write-back modes were missing | `S7B-LIBRARY-001` to `S7B-LIBRARY-006` |
| `data-source-model-config.html` | 38 buttons, 6 inputs: create config version, tabs, edit mode, source status, model weights, thresholds, version audit | Config version tasks existed, but the page controls and source-state toggles were not decomposed | `S7B-CONFIG-001` to `S7B-CONFIG-006` |

All customer-facing pages keep the City Situation header style and Chinese menu labels. The body must first match the static/design baseline, then replace all static data and static handlers with FastAPI/PostgreSQL-backed contracts before freeze.

### 4.3 Overlay, drawer, more-list, and secondary-surface ledger

Frontend scope is not limited to the main HTML page body. Any modal, drawer, popover, lightbox, "more" list, detail panel, export/task panel, approval panel, or secondary page opened from the main page is part of the product surface. It must have its own route or persisted view-state contract, real API source, empty/error/degraded/no-permission states, browser click evidence, network log, console log, screenshot, and third-party review before the parent page can be frozen.

| Parent page | Secondary surfaces that must be implemented | API / DB contract requirement | Freeze requirement |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| City situation | Event detail drawer, data package jump, mainline prompt drawer, current hot rank "more", video/live "more", sentiment "more", new-hot events "more", spread-speed "more", breakout "more", cross-platform "more", source-health "more" | Each surface reads from `/api/v1/cities/*` or object detail APIs; more lists must use backend pagination; open/selection/share actions persist to view-state or audit tables | Every "more" click opens a real React surface, not a toast; screenshot and network log required |
| Topic situation | Related-events more page, all video/live page, candidate-mainline more page, export-report entry, source contribution detail, emotion/stance term detail | Topic surfaces query `/api/v1/topics/*`; report entry creates or opens a persisted report/export run | Parent filters must carry into secondary surfaces and survive refresh |
| Data and signal workbench | Selected-data detail drawer, original material viewer, recommendation detail, similar-data result panel, supplement-run panel, add-to-mainline confirmation | Workbench surfaces query raw/normalized/signal/evidence refs and write draft/supplement/search run rows | No row detail may be assembled from frontend list data only |
| Evidence detail | Evidence-chain detail panel, lineage node drawer, risk-score breakdown, manual-review panel, confirm-to-simulation confirmation, return-to-observation reason panel | Evidence surfaces query evidence/lineage/risk/review tables and write review/adjustment/world-state-input records | Confirm/reject/adjust actions require reason, audit, and conflict handling |
| Mainline builder | Structure drawer, add trigger/pivot/gap/evidence panels, clue-box detail, node/edge detail drawer, view-all candidates page, confirm-with-gaps confirmation, quality issue task panel | Builder surfaces query mainline graph/suggestions/quality issues and write versioned decisions, layout, gap waivers, tasks | Graph UI cannot mutate local state without a persisted mainline version |
| Worldline observer | Council start modal, node detail drawer, intervention panel, hypothesis branch confirmation, learn-more Council page, last-result panel | Worldline surfaces query worldline run/step/intervention/Council refs and write branch/intervention/playback/view-state rows | Opening modal, cancel, start, rerun, and save must all be browser-tested |
| Agent Council | Agent/profile detail panel, dialogue transcript drawer, pressure-test result panel, probability/explainability detail, save judgment confirmation, inject-and-rerun confirmation | Council surfaces query agent profile, LLM call, guardrail, evidence, and worldline refs; conclusions write persisted judgment/result rows | No Agent output can be shown without DB record and evidence/input refs |
| Decision brief | Single export panel, batch export panel, create-task panel, claim evidence locator, worldline detail link, Council detail link, document status drawer | Report surfaces query report claims/evidence/exports/tasks and write export/task/audit rows | Export progress, failure, retry, and download availability must be visible |
| Case memory | Review-note detail, task/action detail, model-calibration approval panel, save draft confirmation, submit-review panel, publish-to-memory confirmation, export-sample panel | Retrospective surfaces query reviews/metrics/tasks and write knowledge item, case candidate, calibration dataset records | Memory publish is blocked unless review gate passes |
| Case library | Case detail panel, apply-mode drawer, write-back confirmation, current-topic add panel, simulation-apply panel, sort/filter menu | Library surfaces query case library/search/application draft APIs and write application draft or target object updates after approval | Apply/write-back cannot directly mutate target without draft/version/audit |
| Config center | Config group switch drawer, edit-mode session panel, source state panel, parameter edit panels, pending approval detail, regression result panel, rollback validation panel | Config surfaces query version/config/source/model/prompt APIs and write draft versions, edit sessions, approvals, validations, rollback rows | Every config change is versioned, audited, review-gated, and rollback-testable |

### 4.4 Business capability decomposition ledger

Adopted source: `C:/Users/ROG/Desktop/business-capability-ledger-v1.0.md`.

This section is the business-capability master ledger for the production plan. It complements section 9 engineering atomic tasks and is binding for execution: every engineering task must map to one or more `Dxx-Axx` business actions before implementation and freeze.

Adoption override: any suggestion below to create separate business ledger files is treated as a request to maintain the same content inside this master plan and existing contract artifacts unless the user explicitly asks for separate files. Do not create parallel plan documents by default.

#### 0. 文档定位

本文件用于补齐生产级开发计划中的“业务能力视角”。

`production-plan-v1.0` 已经把系统拆到了工程原子任务、API、DB、工作流、浏览器验收和第三方检查层面；本文件进一步把系统拆成：

```text
业务域
→ 业务对象
→ 业务动作
→ 生命周期状态
→ 页面入口
→ API / Workflow
→ DB 对象
→ 审计对象
→ 测试与冻结条件
```

本文件不是替代开发计划，而是作为开发计划的业务能力总账。后续 AI / Agent 执行时，必须同时参考：

```text
1. production-plan-v1.0-20260509.md
2. 本计划 4.4 Business capability decomposition ledger
3. api-db-contract-v1.0
4. page surface contract
5. review gate contract
```

---

#### 1. 总体业务闭环

完整系统主链路：

```text
城市态势感知
→ 主题态势
→ 数据 / 信号检索
→ 事件 / 证据复核
→ 主线建模确认
→ 世界线推演
→ 多主体研判
→ 汇报输出
→ 复盘知识沉淀
→ 主题 / 案例库
→ 数据源与模型配置
→ 反哺下一次城市态势感知与主线判断
```

核心原则：

```text
1. 不输出确定性结论，只输出概率、趋势、置信度、观察变量和建议动作。
2. 城市页不判断“高低风险”，只完整呈现城市正在发生的事。
3. 先处理情绪，再处理事件。
4. 线上多源信号为主，保留线下反馈与事实校验逻辑。
5. 每个业务判断必须可追溯到原始输入、证据、算法版本、Prompt 版本或人工复核记录。
6. 复盘不是一线用户报告，而是系统学习材料。
7. 所有业务动作必须有 API、DB 记录、审计日志和第三方检查记录。
```

---

#### 2. 业务域总览

| 域编号 | 业务域 | 核心对象 | 主要页面 | 业务目的 |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| D01 | 城市事件发现域 | CityEvent | 城市态势感知页 | 发现城市里正在发生什么 |
| D02 | 主题聚合域 | Topic | 主题态势页 | 把热点聚合成可观察主题 |
| D03 | 数据 / 信号工作台域 | Signal / SignalPackage | 数据 / 信号检索页 | 汇集可解释热度、情绪、传播和主线的信号 |
| D04 | 证据复核域 | Evidence / EvidenceReview | 事件 / 证据复核页 | 判断信号是否可靠、是否可进入主线 |
| D05 | 主线建模域 | Mainline / WorldStateInput | 主线建模确认页 | 把信号组织成可推演主线 |
| D06 | 世界线推演域 | WorldlineRun / ResponseAction | 世界线推演页 | 推演回应动作如何影响情绪、传播和破圈 |
| D07 | 多主体研判域 | CouncilSession / StakeholderReaction | Agent Council 页 | 压力测试各方对处置动作的反应 |
| D08 | 汇报输出域 | DecisionBrief / ReportClaim / Task | 汇报输出页 | 形成阶段性研判、建议动作和监测任务 |
| D09 | 复盘知识沉淀域 | CaseMemory / KnowledgeItem | 复盘知识沉淀页 | 把案例沉淀成系统学习材料 |
| D10 | 主题 / 案例库域 | CaseLibraryEntry / PatternTemplate | 主题 / 案例库页 | 支持相似案例召回与模板复用 |
| D11 | 数据源与模型配置域 | DataSource / ModelConfig | 配置中心页 | 管理数据源、权重、阈值、Agent 与发布 |
| D12 | 任务与通知域 | Task / Notification | 任务中心 / 顶部通知 | 承接后续处理、监测和审批待办 |
| D13 | 审批与第三方检查域 | ReviewGate | Review / Gate 页面 | 所有关键输出发布前审查 |
| D14 | 可追溯与解释域 | Lineage / Explanation | 所有详情页 | 让结论回到证据、输入、算法和配置 |
| D15 | 运维与观测域 | WorkflowRun / OpsMetric | Ops 页面 | 保证采集、算法、LLM、工作流可监控 |

---

#### D01. 城市事件发现域

#### D01.1 业务定位

城市事件发现域负责回答：

```text
这个城市现在发生了什么？
哪些事件正在升温？
哪里有视频、直播、评论、同城讨论？
哪些事件值得进入主题观察？
```

城市页只呈现热度、传播、同城讨论、视频 / 直播、来源和变化，不替用户做最终风险判断。

#### D01.2 业务对象

| 对象 | 说明 |
|---|---|
| City | 城市对象 |
| CityRegion | 城市区域 / 区县 / 街道 |
| CityEvent | 城市事件 |
| CityMapLayer | 地图图层 |
| CityEventCluster | 地图聚合点 |
| CityEventHeatCell | 热力图单元 |
| CityTimelineItem | 城市时间线项 |
| CitySourceHealth | 城市数据源健康摘要 |
| CityViewState | 城市页视图状态 |

#### D01.3 生命周期状态

###### CityEvent 状态

```text
candidate
observing
active
selected
converted_to_topic
sent_to_review
noise
archived
```

###### CityViewState 状态

```text
loading
normal
```

#### D02. 主题聚合域

#### D02.1 业务定位

主题聚合域负责把一个或多个城市热点组织成“可持续观察的主题”。

它回答：

```text
这个热点是否已经形成主题？
主题由哪些信号组成？
传播阶段是什么？
同城情绪和主要诉求是什么？
是否出现破圈苗头？
是否产生候选主线？
```

#### D02.2 业务对象

| 对象 | 说明 |
|---|---|
| Topic | 主题 |
| TopicSourceBreakdown | 主题来源构成 |
| TopicTrend | 主题热度 / 讨论趋势 |
| TopicSpreadPath | 传播路径 |
| TopicEmotionStance | 情绪 / 立场分析 |
| TopicCandidateMainline | 候选主线 |
| TopicViewState | 主题页视图状态 |

#### D02.3 生命周期状态

###### Topic 状态

```text
candidate
observing
active
merged
split
archived
converted_to_mainline
```

###### TopicCandidateMainline 状态

```text
candidate
recommended
selected
sent_to_mainline_builder
discarded
```

#### D02.4 业务动作

| ID | 业务动作 | 用户 / 系统动作 | API / Workflow | DB 对象 | 审计 |
|---|---|---|---|---|---|

| D02-A02 | 查询主题列表 | 用户动作 | `GET /api/v1/topics` | `topics` | 否 |
| D02-A03 | 加载主题态势页 | 系统动作 | `GET /api/v1/topics/{id}/situation-view` | `topics`, `signals` | 否 |
| D02-A04 | 切换主题时间窗口 | 用户动作 | `PATCH /api/v1/topics/{id}/view-state` | `topic_view_states` | 是 |
| D02-A05 | 查看主题来源构成 | 用户动作 | `GET /api/v1/topics/{id}/source-breakdown` | `signals` | 否 |
| D02-A06 | 查看热度趋势 | 用户动作 | `GET /api/v1/topics/{id}/trends` | `topic_trends` | 否 |

#### D03. 数据 / 信号工作台域

#### D03.1 业务定位

数据 / 信号工作台用于围绕一个主题查找、筛选、比较、汇集信号。

它回答：

```text
哪些数据能解释这个主题为什么升温？
哪些视频、直播、评论、图文、热线、公告可以支撑主线？
哪些信号只是噪声？
哪些信号需要送证据复核？
```

#### D03.2 业务对象

| 对象 | 说明 |
|---|---|
| RawRecord | 原始记录 |
| NormalizedRecord | 清洗记录 |
| Signal | 信号 |
| SignalPackage | 信号草稿包 |
| SignalPackageItem | 草稿包内信号 |
| SimilarSignalResult | 相似信号结果 |
| SignalSearchRun | 检索运行记录 |
| SignalWorkbenchView | 工作台聚合视图 |

#### D03.3 生命周期状态

```text

```

```text

```

---

#### D04. 证据复核域

#### D04.1 业务定位

证据复核域负责判断信号能不能作为主线依据。

复核不是只判断“真假”，而是同时判断：

```text
1. 内容真实性
2. 情绪 / 立场代表性
3. 传播影响
4. 是否可进入主线
5. 是否只能作为概率参考
```

#### D04.2 业务对象

| 对象 | 说明 |
|---|---|
| Evidence | 证据 |
| EvidenceReview | 证据复核任务 |
| EvidenceClaim | 证据声明 |
| EvidenceMediaLink | 媒体证据链接 |
| SourceChain | 来源链 |
| TruthReview | 内容真实性复核 |
| EmotionReview | 情绪代表性复核 |
| SpreadReview | 传播影响复核 |

#### D04.3 生命周期状态

###### Evidence 状态

```text
candidate
needs_review
truth_reviewing
emotion_reviewing
spread_reviewing
confirmed
rejected
probability_reference_only
used_in_mainline
archived
```

#### D04.4 业务动作

| ID | 业务动作 | 用户 / 系统动作 | API / Workflow | DB 对象 | 审计 |
|---|---|---|---|---|---|
| D04-A01 | 创建证据复核任务 | 用户动作 | `POST /api/v1/evidence-reviews` | `evidence_reviews` | 是 |
| D04-A02 | 加载复核页 | 系统动作 | `GET /api/v1/evidence-reviews/{id}/review-view` | `evidence`, `evidence_reviews` | 否 |
| D04-A03 | 查看原始内容 | 用户动作 | `GET /api/v1/evidence/{id}/raw-content` | `raw_records` | 否 |
| D04-A04 | 查看来源链 | 用户动作 | `GET /api/v1/evidence/{id}/source-chain` | `lineage_edges` | 否 |
| D04-A05 | 内容真实性复核 | 用户动作 | `PATCH /api/v1/evidence/{id}/truth-review` | `evidence_reviews` | 是 |
| D04-A06 | 情绪代表性复核 | 用户动作 | `PATCH /api/v1/evidence/{id}/emotion-review` | `evidence_reviews` | 是 |
| D04-A07 | 传播影响复核 | 用户动作 | `PATCH /api/v1/evidence/{id}/spread-review` | `evidence_reviews` | 是 |
| D04-A08 | 标记可用证据 | 用户动作 | `PATCH /api/v1/evidence/{id}/review` | `evidence` | 是 |
| D04-A09 | 标记待复核 | 用户动作 | `PATCH /api/v1/evidence/{id}/review` | `evidence` | 是 |

| D04-A11 | 标记仅作概率参考 | 用户动作 | `PATCH /api/v1/evidence/{id}/review` | `evidence` | 是 |
| D04-A12 | 上传补充材料 | 用户动作 | `POST /api/v1/evidence/{id}/attachments` | `media_assets` | 是 |
| D04-A13 | 绑定媒体证据 | 用户动作 | `POST /api/v1/evidence/{id}/media-links` | `evidence_media_links` | 是 |
| D04-A14 | 进入主线建模 | 用户动作 | `POST /api/v1/mainlines/drafts` | `mainlines` | 是 |

#### D05. 主线建模域

#### D05.1 业务定位

主线建模域负责把可用信号、证据、情绪、诉求和扩散路径组织成可推演结构。

核心产物：

```text
已确认主线
+ 关键不确定性
+ World State 输入包
```

#### D05.2 业务对象

| 对象 | 说明 |
|---|---|
| Mainline | 主线 |
| MainlineVersion | 主线版本 |
| MainlineNode | 主线节点 |
| MainlineEdge | 主线边 |
| MainlineQualityGate | 主线质量检查 |
| WorldStateInput | 推演输入包 |
| UncertaintyVariable | 不确定性变量 |

#### D05.3 生命周期状态

###### Mainline 状态

```text
draft
quality_failed
pending_confirmation
confirmed
world_state_generated
archived
```

###### MainlineNode 类型

```text
signal_cluster
emotion_need
narrative
spread_path
uncertainty
candidate_mainline
world_state_input
```

| D05-A03 | 生成信号簇节点 | 系统动作 | `POST /api/v1/mainlines/{id}/generate-signal-clusters` | `mainline_nodes` | 是 |
| D05-A04 | 生成情绪 / 诉求节点 | 系统动作 | `POST /api/v1/mainlines/{id}/generate-emotion-needs` | `mainline_nodes` | 是 |
| D05-A05 | 生成主叙事节点 | 系统动作 | `POST /api/v1/mainlines/{id}/generate-narrative` | `mainline_nodes` | 是 |

#### D06. 世界线推演域

#### D06.1 业务定位

世界线推演域负责推演不同回应动作对情绪、传播、破圈和主叙事的影响。

它不是“预测唯一未来”，而是生成多条可能路径。

#### D06.2 业务对象

| 对象 | 说明 |
|---|---|
| WorldState | 世界状态 |
| WorldlineRun | 推演运行 |
| WorldlineNode | 世界线节点 |
| WorldlineEdge | 节点边 |
| ResponseAction | 处置 / 回应动作 |
| WorldlineBranch | A/B/C/D 分支 |
| WorldlineVersion | 推演版本 |

#### D06.3 生命周期状态

###### WorldlineRun 状态

```text
pending
running
completed
failed
canceled
superseded
```

###### ResponseAction 状态

```text
candidate
injected
simulated
applied_to_council
discarded
```

#### D06.4 业务动作

| ID | 业务动作 | 用户 / 系统动作 | API / Workflow | DB 对象 | 审计 |
|---|---|---|---|---|---|
| D06-A01 | 创建推演运行 | 用户动作 | `POST /api/v1/worldline-runs` | `worldline_runs` | 是 |
| D06-A02 | 加载推演页 | 系统动作 | `GET /api/v1/worldline-runs/{id}/simulation-view` | `worldline_runs` | 否 |
| D06-A03 | 生成初始节点 | 系统动作 | `GenerateWorldlineWorkflow` | `worldline_nodes` | 是 |
| D06-A04 | 生成回应动作候选 | 系统动作 | `GenerateWorldlineWorkflow` | `worldline_interventions` | 是 |
| D06-A05 | 计算分支概率 | 系统动作 | `GenerateWorldlineWorkflow` | `worldline_nodes` | 是 |
| D06-A06 | 查看节点详情 | 用户动作 | `GET /api/v1/worldline-nodes/{id}` | `worldline_nodes` | 否 |
| D06-A07 | 注入处置动作 | 用户动作 | `POST /api/v1/worldline-runs/{id}/interventions` | `worldline_interventions` | 是 |
| D06-A08 | 自定义处置动作 | 用户动作 | `POST /api/v1/worldline-runs/{id}/interventions` | `worldline_interventions` | 是 |

---

#### D07. 多主体研判域

#### D07.1 业务定位

多主体研判不是“开会”，而是对一个处置动作进行压力测试。

它回答：

```text
当事群体会不会接受？
同城群众会如何理解？
媒体/自媒体会如何解读？
平台机制会不会继续放大？
属地和主管部门动作是否匹配？
世界线分支概率应该如何校准？
```

#### D07.2 业务对象

| 对象 | 说明 |
|---|---|
| Stakeholder | 利益方 |
| AgentProfile | Agent 画像 |
| CouncilSession | 研判会话 |
| CouncilMessage | 单 Agent 输出 |
| CouncilResult | 研判结果 |
| StakeholderReaction | 主体反应 |
| BlockedClaim | 被阻断声明 |

#### D07.3 生命周期状态

###### CouncilSession 状态

```text
created
profile_checking
running
schema_validating
blocked
completed
applied
```

###### AgentProfile 状态

```text
draft
user_md_generated
soul_md_generated
agent_md_generated
review_pending
ready
rejected
archived
```

#### D07.4 业务动作

| ID | 业务动作 | 用户 / 系统动作 | API / Workflow | DB 对象 | 审计 |
|---|---|---|---|---|---|
| D07-A01 | 识别利益方 | 系统动作 | `POST /api/v1/case-graphs/{case_id}/stakeholders` | `stakeholders` | 是 |
| D07-A02 | 生成 Agent Profile | 系统动作 | `POST /api/v1/agent-profiles/generate` | `agent_profiles` | 是 |
| D07-A03 | 生成 user.md | 系统动作 | `POST /api/v1/agent-profiles/{id}/user-md` | `agent_profile_files` | 是 |
| D07-A04 | 生成 soul.md | 系统动作 | `POST /api/v1/agent-profiles/{id}/soul-md` | `agent_profile_files` | 是 |
| D07-A05 | 生成 agent.md | 系统动作 | `POST /api/v1/agent-profiles/{id}/agent-md` | `agent_profile_files` | 是 |
| D07-A06 | Agent Profile 审核 | 用户动作 | `POST /api/v1/reviews` | `reviews` | 是 |

| D07-A08 | 运行 Council | 用户动作 | `POST /api/v1/council-sessions/{id}/run` | `council_messages` | 是 |
| D07-A09 | 单 Agent schema 校验 | 系统动作 | `RunCouncilWorkflow` | `council_messages` | 是 |
| D07-A10 | blocked claims 检查 | 系统动作 | `RunCouncilWorkflow` | `blocked_claims` | 是 |

| D07-A13 | 分支概率变化计算 | 系统动作 | `RunCouncilWorkflow` | `council_results` | 是 |
| D07-A14 | Council Result 审查 | 用户动作 | `POST /api/v1/reviews` | `reviews` | 是 |
| D07-A15 | 回写世界线 | 用户动作 | `POST /api/v1/council-sessions/{id}/apply` | `worldline_runs` | 是 |

#### D07.5 StakeholderReaction 字段

```text

```

#### D08. 汇报输出域

#### D08.1 业务定位

汇报输出域负责把前面所有结果整理为阶段性判断和建议动作。

它不输出最终定性，只输出：

```text
概率判断
趋势变化
置信度
建议动作
不确定性说明
后续观察变量
任务建议
```

#### D08.2 业务对象

| 对象 | 说明 |
|---|---|

| Report | 报告 |
| ReportVersion | 报告版本 |
| ReportClaim | 报告声明 |
| ReportExport | 报告导出 |
| Task | 任务 |
| TaskEvent | 任务事件 |

#### D08.3 生命周期状态

```text

published

archived
```

###### ReportClaim 状态

```text
draft

published
```

#### D09. 复盘知识沉淀域

#### D09.1 业务定位

复盘沉淀域服务系统学习，不服务一线最终处置。

它回答：

```text
这次判断哪里命中了？
哪里偏差了？
哪些前因信号应该增强？
哪些噪声应该降权？
哪些处置动作有效？
哪些模式应进入案例库？
```

#### D09.2 业务对象

| 对象 | 说明 |
|---|---|
| Retrospective | 复盘 |
| CaseMemory | 案例记忆 |
| KnowledgeItem | 知识项 |
| PredictionComparison | 预测对比 |
| ModelCalibrationSuggestion | 模型校准建议 |
| MisjudgementSample | 误判样本 |

#### D09.3 生命周期状态

###### Retrospective 状态

```text
draft
case_data_missing
prediction_not_comparable
review_pending
review_failed
approved_for_memory
published_to_case_library
archived
```

###### KnowledgeItem 状态

```text
draft
pending_review
approved
published
rejected
superseded
```

#### D09.4 业务动作

| ID | 业务动作 | 用户 / 系统动作 | API / Workflow | DB 对象 | 审计 |
|---|---|---|---|---|---|
| D09-A01 | 创建复盘 | 用户动作 | `POST /api/v1/retrospectives` | `retrospectives` | 是 |
| D09-A02 | 加载复盘页 | 系统动作 | `GET /api/v1/retrospectives/{id}/memory-view` | `retrospectives` | 否 |
| D09-A03 | 录入实际结果 | 用户动作 | `PATCH /api/v1/retrospectives/{id}/actual-result` | `retrospectives` | 是 |
| D09-A04 | 预测路径对比 | 系统动作 | `POST /api/v1/retrospectives/{id}/compare` | `case_memories` | 是 |
| D09-A05 | 标注偏差类型 | 用户动作 | `PATCH /api/v1/retrospectives/{id}/bias-labels` | `case_memories` | 是 |
| D09-A06 | 生成前因模板 | 系统动作 | `POST /api/v1/knowledge-items` | `knowledge_items` | 是 |
| D09-A07 | 生成处置动作效果 | 系统动作 | `POST /api/v1/knowledge-items` | `knowledge_items` | 是 |
| D09-A08 | 生成误判样本 | 系统动作 | `POST /api/v1/knowledge-items` | `knowledge_items` | 是 |

| D09-A12 | 发布到案例库 | 用户动作 | `POST /api/v1/case-library-entries` | `case_library_entries` | 是 |

#### D11.4 ConfigImpactAnalysis 必答项

```text
影响哪些页面？
影响哪些模型？
影响哪些历史案例？
是否改变报告结论？
是否需要回归测试？
是否需要灰度发布？
是否允许回滚？
```

#### D13. 审批与第三方检查域

#### D13.1 业务定位

第三方检查是系统门禁，不是口头流程。

任何关键输出在冻结、发布、回写、导出、配置生效前，都必须有独立检查记录。

#### D13.2 可检查对象

```text
API
DataSource
AlgorithmOutput
MediaOutput
AgentProfile
CouncilResult
Report
FrontendPage
ConfigVersion
KnowledgeItem
```

#### D13.3 ReviewGate 生命周期

```text
pending
pass
fail
waived
retest_pending
closed
```

#### D13.4 业务动作

| ID | 业务动作 | API |
|---|---|
| D13-A01 | 创建检查任务 | `POST /api/v1/reviews` |
| D13-A02 | 查询检查任务 | `GET /api/v1/reviews` |
| D13-A03 | 查看检查详情 | `GET /api/v1/reviews/{id}` |
| D13-A04 | 提交通过 | `PATCH /api/v1/reviews/{id}` |
| D13-A05 | 提交失败 | `PATCH /api/v1/reviews/{id}` |
| D13-A06 | 创建修复任务 | `POST /api/v1/reviews/{id}/fix-task` |
| D13-A07 | 复测 | `POST /api/v1/reviews/{id}/retest` |
| D13-A08 | 豁免 | `POST /api/v1/reviews/{id}/waive` |
| D13-A09 | 门禁检查 | `POST /api/v1/reviews/{id}/gate-check` |

---

#### D14. 可追溯与解释域

#### D14.1 业务定位

解释域负责让每个判断都能回到来源。

必须支持：

```text
报告 → 声明 → 证据 → 信号 → 原始数据 → 数据源 → 采集运行
推演 → World State → 主线 → 证据 → 信号
Council → Agent Profile → 利益方 → 图谱 → 证据
配置变更 → 模型结果变化 → 报告影响
```

#### D14.2 业务动作

| ID | 业务动作 | API |
|---|---|
| D14-A01 | 查询对象血缘 | `GET /api/v1/lineage/{object_type}/{object_id}` |
| D14-A02 | 查询证据引用 | `GET /api/v1/evidence/{id}/references` |
| D14-A03 | 查询报告声明引用 | `GET /api/v1/reports/{id}/claims/{claim_id}/evidence` |
| D14-A04 | 查询算法版本 | `GET /api/v1/algorithm-runs/{id}` |
| D14-A05 | 查询 LLM 调用记录 | `GET /api/v1/llm/calls/{id}` |
| D14-A06 | 查询配置影响 | `GET /api/v1/config/releases/{id}/impact` |
| D14-A07 | 生成解释摘要 | `POST /api/v1/explanations` |

---

#### D15. 运维与观测域

#### D15.1 业务定位

运维与观测域保证采集、清洗、算法、LLM、工作流、导出等长任务可监控、可失败归因、可重试、可审计。

#### D15.2 业务对象

| 对象 | 说明 |
|---|---|
| WorkflowRun | 工作流运行 |
| WorkflowRunEvent | 工作流事件 |
| OpsMetric | 运维指标 |
| ErrorQueueItem | 错误队列 |
| RetryQueueItem | 重试队列 |
| HealthStatus | 健康状态 |

#### D15.3 业务动作

| ID | 业务动作 | API |
|---|---|
| D15-A01 | 查询系统健康 | `GET /api/v1/ops/health` |
| D15-A02 | 查询 API 状态 | `GET /api/v1/ops/api-health` |
| D15-A03 | 查询 DB 状态 | `GET /api/v1/ops/db-health` |
| D15-A04 | 查询 Worker 状态 | `GET /api/v1/ops/workers` |
| D15-A05 | 查询 LLM Provider 状态 | `GET /api/v1/llm/providers/status` |
| D15-A06 | 查询工作流运行 | `GET /api/v1/workflow-runs` |
| D15-A07 | 查询错误队列 | `GET /api/v1/ops/error-queue` |
| D15-A08 | 查询重试队列 | `GET /api/v1/ops/retry-queue` |
| D15-A09 | 重试失败任务 | `POST /api/v1/ops/retry-queue/{id}/retry` |
| D15-A10 | 查看成本指标 | `GET /api/v1/ops/costs` |
| D15-A11 | 查看延迟指标 | `GET /api/v1/ops/latency` |

#### 4. 业务对象状态机总表

| 对象 | 状态 |
|---|---|
| CityEvent | candidate / observing / active / selected / converted_to_topic / sent_to_review / noise / archived |
| Topic | candidate / observing / active / merged / split / archived / converted_to_mainline |
| Signal | raw_candidate / selected / in_package / sent_to_review / excluded / archived |
| SignalPackage | draft / collecting / ready_for_review / sent_to_review / partially_reviewed / locked / archived |
| Evidence | candidate / needs_review / truth_reviewing / emotion_reviewing / spread_reviewing / confirmed / rejected / probability_reference_only / used_in_mainline / archived |
| Mainline | draft / quality_failed / pending_confirmation / confirmed / world_state_generated / archived |
| WorldlineRun | pending / running / completed / failed / canceled / superseded |
| ResponseAction | candidate / injected / simulated / applied_to_council / discarded |
| CouncilSession | created / profile_checking / running / schema_validating / blocked / completed / applied |
| AgentProfile | draft / user_md_generated / soul_md_generated / agent_md_generated / review_pending / ready / rejected / archived |
| Report | draft / claim_validation_failed / submitted_review / review_returned / approved / published / exported / archived |
| ReportClaim | draft / evidence_linked / validation_failed / blocked / approved / published |
| Retrospective | draft / case_data_missing / prediction_not_comparable / review_pending / review_failed / approved_for_memory / published_to_case_library / archived |
| KnowledgeItem | draft / pending_review / approved / published / rejected / superseded |
| Task | draft / assigned / accepted / in_progress / blocked / completed / closed / overdue / canceled |
| ReviewGate | pending / pass / fail / waived / retest_pending / closed |

---

#### 5. 横向能力要求

#### 5.1 所有业务动作必须具备

```text
API 或 Workflow
DB 记录
审计日志
错误码
权限判断
状态变更
前端状态
功能测试
异常测试
性能测试
浏览器验证
第三方检查
```

#### 5.2 所有生成型输出必须具备

```text
input_refs
evidence_refs
algorithm_version 或 prompt_version
confidence
status
failure_reason
trace_id
review_gate
blocked_claims
```

适用对象：

```text
Signal
Evidence
RiskFactor
Mainline
WorldState
WorldlineRun
AgentProfile
CouncilResult
Report
KnowledgeItem
ConfigImpactAnalysis
```

#### 5.3 所有页面必须覆盖状态

```text
loading
normal
empty
error
degraded
no_permission
selected
submitting
success
failure
409_conflict
dependency_degraded
```

---

#### 6. AI 执行规则

当 AI / Agent 执行生产计划时，必须按以下顺序理解任务：

```text
1. 先定位业务域
2. 再定位业务对象
3. 再确认业务动作
4. 再确认状态机
5. 再确认页面入口与二级表面
6. 再确认 API / Workflow
7. 再确认 DB 读写
8. 再确认审计与 Review Gate
9. 再开发
10. 再测试与浏览器验证
11. 最后冻结
```

禁止：

```text
1. 只看页面按钮开发功能。
2. 只看 API 列表开发功能。
3. 跳过业务对象状态机。
4. 跳过 Review Gate。
5. 使用前端 mock 假装业务结果。
6. 使用无 DB 记录的 Agent / LLM 输出。
7. 使用无证据引用的报告事实判断。
```

---

#### 7. 与 production-plan-v1.0 的关系

本文件是 `production-plan-v1.0` 的业务能力补充层。

执行时：

```text
production-plan-v1.0
负责工程原子任务、API、DB、测试、浏览器和 review gate。

business-capability-ledger-v1.0
负责解释每个任务属于什么业务域、操作什么业务对象、导致什么业务状态变化、服务哪条业务闭环。
```

两者必须一起使用。

如果两份文档冲突：

```text
1. 生产级约束优先。
2. 数据可追溯优先。
3. 后端真实状态优先。
4. 安全合规优先。
5. 业务闭环完整性优先。
```

---

#### 8. 后续建议

建议后续继续补三类合同，但默认在本主计划和既有合同文件内维护，不新增并行实施计划：

```text
1. business-object-schema
   详细定义每个业务对象字段、关系和状态变更规则。

2. business-action-contract
   将 D01-A01 到 D15-A11 拆成 API、请求体、响应体、错误码、审计、测试。

3. page-surface-business-contract
   将每个页面、抽屉、弹窗、more 列表、详情面板映射到业务动作。
```

---

#### 9. 最终结论

当前系统的业务能力可以继续细分，并建议按本文件形成业务能力总账。

最终系统不只是页面集合，而是：

```text
以城市事件发现为入口，
以主题聚合和信号检索为基础，
以证据复核和主线建模为核心，
以世界线推演和多主体压力测试为研判引擎，
以汇报输出和任务闭环为业务交付，
以复盘知识沉淀、案例库和配置中心反哺系统能力的完整闭环。
```

Immediate S1 OpenAPI/DTO prerequisites before FE-S1 execution:

1. Decide whether `/api/v1/me`, `/api/v1/me/navigation`, and `/api/v1/me/permissions` are canonical, or alias them to the existing `/api/v1/auth/me` and `/api/v1/auth/permissions` paths. The frontend menu/button contract cannot freeze until this is explicit.
2. Add or canonicalize user management mutations required by section 9: `PATCH /api/v1/users/{id}/roles`, `PATCH /api/v1/users/{id}/status`, and `GET /api/v1/audit-logs/{id}`.
3. Add the review-gate API group or document aliases to `/api/v1/reviews`: `POST /api/v1/review-gates`, `GET /api/v1/tasks/{task_id}/review-gates`, `POST /api/v1/review-gates/{id}/retest`, `POST /api/v1/review-checklists/versions`, and release summary `GET /api/v1/release/review-gates-summary`.
4. Resolve Ops path naming before S1 Ops UI work: current OpenAPI uses `/api/v1/ops/health/api`, `/api/v1/ops/health/db`, and `/api/v1/ops/health/workers`; section 4.4/9 expect `/api/v1/ops/api-health`, `/api/v1/ops/db-health`, `/api/v1/ops/workers`, and `/api/v1/ops/health`.
5. Add DTOs for S0/S1 contract objects that are currently only implicit or generic: `PageSurfaceContract`, `PageViewState`, `BrowserVerificationRecord`, `BusinessCapabilityContract`, `BusinessStateMachine`, `BusinessFlowEdge`, `DecisionPoint`, `WriteBackPoint`, `BusinessQualityGate`, `ATTraceabilityRow`, `ReviewGateRecord`, `ReviewChecklistVersion`, `NavigationItem`, and `ButtonPermissionState`.

Status 2026-05-09: FE-S1 OpenAPI/DTO readiness is complete. `/api/v1/me`, `/api/v1/me/navigation`, `/api/v1/me/permissions`, user role/status mutations, audit detail, review-gate aliases, review-checklist version, release review-gate summary, and Ops aliases are implemented in FastAPI and OpenAPI; legacy `/api/v1/auth/*` and old Ops health paths remain accepted as compatibility aliases. Remaining D13-A06/D13-A07 original `/reviews` mutations and D15-A05/A09/A10/A11 are deferred-not-for-FE-S1 follow-ups.

### 6.1 Alembic gap list

Snapshot source: section 8.1 traceability matrix, section 9 AT ledger, `apps/api/src/worldline_api/models.py`, and `apps/api/alembic/versions`.

Current evidence:

| Evidence | Count / state | Meaning |
| --- | ---: | --- |
| SQLAlchemy model tables in `models.py` | 94 | Current runtime model baseline covers core S1-S7B entities plus S1 contract/review traceability persistence. |
| Alembic revision files present | 14 files: `20260508_0001` through `20260509_0014` | `20260509_0014_contract_review_traceability` exists as the S1 forward gap revision. |
| Planned gap revisions now required | 0015 through 0019 | The previous indexes-only `0014` plan is superseded; indexes move after missing later-stage page-state tables. |
| SQLite Alembic upgrade to head | pass through `20260509_0014` | Full `alembic upgrade head` passed after test-proven SQLite batch-alter fixes in `0010` and `0012`. |

Resolution rules:

1. Preserve existing revision order through `20260509_0013`; do not reorder or rewrite earlier revisions unless a test proves a migration defect.
2. Add forward-only gap revisions before the final indexes/views revision.
3. Do not seed product runtime data in migrations. Seed only reference permissions/templates through idempotent seed commands.
4. Every new table must include tenant/object scoping, status/version where applicable, audit/write-back linkage, and review gate evidence if it can freeze or publish a business object.

| Proposed revision | Missing objects / table groups | Required by | S1/S-stage impact |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |

Immediate Alembic prerequisites before FE-S1 execution:

1. Add `review_gate_records` and `review_checklist_versions`, or explicitly map `AT-360` to existing `reviews` / `review_results` with no separate table. The current section 9 wording requires a separate table, so the default is to add it.
2. Add `page_surface_contracts`, `page_view_states`, and `browser_verification_records` so S0-UI rows can store surface inventory, state matrix, and browser evidence.
3. Add `business_capability_contracts`, `business_state_machines`, `business_flow_edges`, `decision_points`, `write_back_points`, and `business_quality_gates` so S0-BIZ rows have persistence rather than only markdown.
4. Add `file_objects` and `notifications` for S0/S1 upload/export evidence and top notification/task handoff.
5. Add `algorithm_runs` before algorithm-backed pages freeze; if not in the S1 patch, explicitly mark it as deferred but keep `S0` contract tests aware of the gap.

Status 2026-05-09: FE-S1 Alembic readiness is complete. `20260509_0014_contract_review_traceability` adds review gate records, checklist versions, page/browser evidence, business contract ledgers, file objects, notifications, and algorithm runs; model metadata detects 94 tables and SQLite `alembic upgrade head` reaches `0014`.

## 7. Algorithm / workflow / Agent ledger

| Stage | Required real implementation group |
| --- | --- |
| S2 | parser, cleaner, normalizer, dedupe, data quality, source policy, collection workflow, retry/dead-letter/cursor |
| S4A | LLM field mapping, extraction, JSON repair, schema validation, evidence boundary, signal generation/scoring |
| S4B | evidence candidates, risk factor generation/scoring, conflict detection, OCR/ASR/VLM/media processing, redaction, cross-modal corroboration |
| S5 | mainline node/edge generation, quality scoring, world state, case graph, stakeholder discovery |
| S6 | worldline simulation/rerun/compare/explain, LLM provider/budget/invoke, profile user.md/soul.md/agent.md, council aggregation, guardrails, counterfactual/replay/eval |
| S7A | report outline/sections, claim/citation validation, export, task generation |
| S7B | case candidate/search/retrieval, config impact, taxonomy/algorithm/agent/prompt regression |

Every run must persist version, input snapshot, output snapshot, evidence_refs/input_refs, blocked_claims, confidence/status/failure_reason, and trace_id.

## 8. Test / business / performance / browser / third-party review ledger

| Test class | Required coverage |
| --- | --- |
| functional | public API/service behavior, DB writes, state transitions, audit, trace_id |
| exception | 400/401/403/404/409/422/429/500/503, dependency failure, schema invalid, provider timeout, duplicate submit, no result, degraded |
| business | Xian synthetic social-issue full chain from raw record to report/task/retrospective/library/config |
| performance | API p95, DB list pagination, workflow concurrency, LLM/media duration, frontend first paint, map/list interaction |
| browser | real click with Playwright or in-app browser, network, console, desktop/mobile screenshots |
| security/compliance | tenant isolation, RBAC, secret masking, sensitive redaction, synthetic watermark, forbidden data policy, evidence-bounded conclusions |
| visual regression | static design/page baseline first, city-situation header style, Chinese menu labels, routeable states screenshot diff |
| third-party review | review_gate_records before freeze; implementer cannot self-approve; failed creates fix task; retest before freeze |

### 8.1 Dxx-Axx to AT traceability matrix

This matrix is the first execution artifact for section 11. It binds the section 4.4 business action ledger to section 9 engineering AT rows before OpenAPI/DTO, Alembic, and S1 execution work begins.

Rules:

1. Every `Dxx-Axx` row must map to at least one section 9 AT row or an explicit `gap-check(...)` marker.
2. `gap-check(...)` means the business action is semantically covered by nearby AT rows, but the exact API/DTO/Alembic contract must be reconciled in the next OpenAPI/DTO or Alembic gap pass before implementation.
3. `RG-STD` means `S0-BIZ-007` + `AT-360` to `AT-365` + `AT-367` + the mapped AT row's third-party PASS requirement. Implementers cannot self-approve.
4. Test profile codes below point to the mapped AT row functional/business/performance-browser columns plus the named S8 cross-stage checks.

| Test profile | Required evidence baseline |
| --- | --- |
| `TEST-S3A-CITY` | S3A functional/exception/browser evidence, desktop/mobile/network/console/screenshots, S8 `AT-245`, `AT-260`, `AT-261`, and map/performance checks when applicable. |
| `TEST-S3B-TOPIC` | S3B functional/exception/browser evidence plus S8 `AT-249`, `AT-260`, `AT-261`, `AT-262`. |
| `TEST-S4A-SIGNAL` | S4A functional/exception/business-flow evidence plus S8 `AT-246`, `AT-247`, `AT-248`, `AT-262`. |

## 9. Full atomic task ledger

Each row is a dispatchable atomic task. If a row is still splittable into create/edit/delete/state/detail/list/retry/export/error/permission/audit/performance/browser/review actions, split it here before implementation.

| Stage | Task count | Objective |
| --- | ---: | --- |
| S0 | 27 | contract freeze: objects, API, DB, permissions, audit, state machines, page contracts |
| S1 | 23 | foundation platform: auth, RBAC, audit, review, workflow run, ops, review gates |
| S2 | 90 | sources, adapters, collection, parsing, cleaning, synthetic Xian samples, media ingest |
| S3A | 39 | Xian city situation page freeze |
| S3B | 16 | topic situation page freeze |
| S4A | 24 | signal extraction and data/signal workbench |
| S4B | 61 | evidence review and multimodal evidence closure |
| S5 | 26 | mainline, world state, stakeholder discovery |
| S6 | 74 | worldline, agent profile, council, LLM guardrails |
| S7A | 26 | report, approval, export, task closure |
| S7B | 41 | retrospective, case library, config center |
| S8 | 21 | end-to-end integration, performance, security, visual regression, release acceptance |

| ID | Priority | Type | Atomic function | Backend API / Workflow / Service | DB / persistence | Algorithm / Agent implementation | Frontend page / scenario | Functional test | Business / exception test | Performance / browser / third-party check | Source section |

## 10. Atomic execution loop

1. Read the atomic task row in section 9.
2. Bind it to the business capability ledger: domain, object, action, state, flow transition, decision point, write-back point, and quality gate.
3. Split further first if it still contains multiple business actions, states, decisions, write-backs, or quality gates.
4. Split further again if it can still be decomposed into engineering actions such as create, edit, delete, list, detail, retry, export, permission, audit, performance, or browser checks.
5. Update OpenAPI / DTO / Schema contract.
6. Update Alembic migration, DB constraints, audit, lineage, state machine, or config version.
7. Implement backend API/service/workflow/activity/algorithm/Agent/LLM guardrail.
8. Add backend unit, integration, business-flow, and state-transition tests.
9. Implement React page/component/surface with real API and required states.
10. Run functional, exception, business, performance, and browser checks.
11. Capture network, console, desktop screenshot, mobile screenshot, and surface screenshot when applicable.
12. Create third-party review record, fix failures, retest, then freeze.

### 11.1 S1 readiness gate checklist

S1 execution is not open until every row in the OpenAPI/DTO and Alembic readiness tables below is complete. A row is complete only when the contract is implemented or the alias/defer decision is explicitly recorded in this main plan and referenced by the changed artifact. FE-S1 work must not start from implicit assumptions.

| Gate | Required decision / change | Completion evidence | Status |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `S1-OPENAPI-001` current-user path policy | Decide whether `/api/v1/me`, `/api/v1/me/navigation`, and `/api/v1/me/permissions` are canonical, or explicit aliases to `/api/v1/auth/me` and `/api/v1/auth/permissions`. | OpenAPI paths or aliases exist; FastAPI route behavior matches; frontend API client uses only the canonical names; section 5.1 is updated if the decision changes counts. | done 2026-05-09 |
| `S1-OPENAPI-002` user admin mutations | Add or canonicalize `PATCH /api/v1/users/{id}/roles`, `PATCH /api/v1/users/{id}/status`, and `GET /api/v1/audit-logs/{id}`. | OpenAPI operations, request/response DTOs, status/error codes, audit fields, and API tests are present. | done 2026-05-09 |
| `S1-OPENAPI-003` review-gate aliases | Add review-gate API group or document aliases to `/api/v1/reviews` for create/list-by-task/retest/checklist-version/release-summary behavior. | `POST /api/v1/review-gates`, `GET /api/v1/tasks/{task_id}/review-gates`, `POST /api/v1/review-gates/{id}/retest`, `POST /api/v1/review-checklists/versions`, and `GET /api/v1/release/review-gates-summary` are implemented or explicitly aliased. | done 2026-05-09 |
| `S1-OPENAPI-004` Ops path naming | Resolve `/api/v1/ops/api-health`, `/api/v1/ops/db-health`, `/api/v1/ops/workers`, and `/api/v1/ops/health` versus existing `/api/v1/ops/health/api`, `/api/v1/ops/health/db`, and `/api/v1/ops/health/workers`. | Canonical/alias policy is visible in OpenAPI; route tests prove both accepted aliases or only the canonical form; FE-S1 Ops surface uses the selected path names. | done 2026-05-09 |
| `S1-OPENAPI-005` S0/S1 DTO surface | Add DTO schemas for page-surface, page-state, browser evidence, business capability/state/flow/decision/write-back/gate, AT traceability, review gate, checklist version, navigation item, and button permission state. | `PageSurfaceContract`, `PageViewState`, `BrowserVerificationRecord`, `BusinessCapabilityContract`, `BusinessStateMachine`, `BusinessFlowEdge`, `DecisionPoint`, `WriteBackPoint`, `BusinessQualityGate`, `ATTraceabilityRow`, `ReviewGateRecord`, `ReviewChecklistVersion`, `NavigationItem`, and `ButtonPermissionState` are present in OpenAPI/DTOs and generated client types. | done 2026-05-09 |

## 12. Document governance

1. Do not create new parallel implementation-plan or backlog files.
2. Any plan change edits this file directly.
3. Stage completion reports may live under docs/reviews but cannot replace this execution entry.
4. When a task gap is found, update section 9 rather than creating another backlog.
5. Default decisions must be recorded in docs/assumptions.md or an ADR and referenced from this file.
